[19] thinking: **Evaluating URL parameters**

I realized that the direct URL didn't apply a category but rather sorted the items. I need to filter for Macs with a capacity greater than 2TB, focusing only on external hard drives. It seems it didn't work as expected. I need to understand the parameters better. Using hrefs sounds helpful, and I can extract them from the filters. I should be able to use DOM evaluate with exact selectors. It might be valuable to inspect the links through console log for external drives, capacity, and Mac compatibility.

[20] tool_call: repl("Extracting filter URLs")
<request>
const links1 = await page.locator('a').evaluateAll(els => els.map(a => ({text:(a.textContent||'').trim().replace(/\s+/g,' '), href:a.href})).filter(x => /External Hard Drives|Mac\s*\(|4TB to|2TB to|6TB to|8TB to|12TB and More|Lowest Price|Price/.test(x.text)) );
console.log(JSON.stringify(links1, null, 2));
</request>

[27] tool_call: repl("Extracting current result data")
<request>
const extractMicroCenterPage1 = await page.evaluate(() => {
  const selected = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('a')).map(a=>a.textContent?.trim().replace(/\s+/g,' ')).filter(t => t && /^(external hard drive|External Hard Drives|Mac)$/.test(t));
  const url = location.href;
  const candidates = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('li, article, .product_wrapper, .product, .result, [class*=product], [class*=result]'))
    .map(el => ({tag: el.tagName, cls: el.className?.toString(), text: el.innerText?.trim().replace(/\s+/g,' ').slice(0,500)}))
    .filter(x => /SKU:|Our price|Original price/.test(x.text||''))
    .slice(0,40);
  return {url, selected, candidates};
});
console.log(JSON.stringify(extractMicroCenterPage1, null, 2));

[29] tool_call: repl("Extracting products from both result pages")
<request>
async function extractProductsCurrentPageMC() {
  return await page.evaluate(() => {
    const moneyToNum = s => s ? Number(s.replace(/[^0-9.]/g,'')) : null;
    const pickTitleLink = (links) => {
      const cleaned = links.map(a => ({text:(a.textContent||'').trim().replace(/\s+/g,' '), href:a.href})).filter(x => x.text && !/^|QUICK VIEW|ADD TO|Compare|\d\.\d out/.test(x.text));
      // Prefer product detail link in result_right, usually the longest title-ish link.
      cleaned.sort((a,b)=>b.text.length-a.text.length);
      return cleaned[0] || {text:'', href:''};
    };
    return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('li.product_wrapper')).map(li => {
      const txt = li.innerText.replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim();
      const titleLink = pickTitleLink(Array.from(li.querySelectorAll('a')));
      const sku = (txt.match(/SKU:\s*([0-9]+)/i)||[])[1] || (txt.match(/SKU\s+([0-9]+)/i)||[])[1] || '';
      const priceMatch = txt.match(/Our price\s*(\$[0-9,]+\.\d{2}|Free|Add to Cart to see price)/i);
      const originalMatch = txt.match(/Original price\s*(\$[0-9,]+\.\d{2})/i);
      const ratingMatch = txt.match(/\b([1-5]\.\d)\s+(?:AVAILABLE|Usually|In Store|Original|Our price)/i) || txt.match(/([1-5]\.\d) out of 5 stars/i);
      return {
        sku,
        title: titleLink.text.replace(/;$/, ''),
        href: titleLink.href,
        priceText: priceMatch ? priceMatch[1] : '',
        price: priceMatch && priceMatch[1].startsWith('$') ? moneyToNum(priceMatch[1]) : (priceMatch && /Free/i.test(priceMatch[1]) ? 0 : null),
        originalPrice: originalMatch ? originalMatch[1] : '',
        availability: /AVAILABLE FOR IN-STORE PICKUP ONLY/i.test(txt) ? 'In-store pickup only' : (/Usually ships in 5-7 business days/i.test(txt) ? 'Ships in 5-7 business days' : (/In Store Only/i.test(txt) ? 'In store only' : '')),
        rating: ratingMatch ? ratingMatch[1] : '',
        raw: txt.slice(0,1000)
      };
    });
  });
}
const baseMC = 'https://www.microcenter.com/search/search_results.aspx?fq=category_flat:External+Hard+Drives|514,Platform:Mac&Ntt=external+hard+drive&sortby=pricelow';
await page.goto(baseMC + '&page=1');
const productsPage1MC = await extractProductsCurrentPageMC();
await page.goto(baseMC + '&page=2');
const productsPage2MC = await extractProductsCurrentPageMC();
const allProductsMC = [...productsPage1MC, ...productsPage2MC];
const parsedMC = allProductsMC.map(p => {
  const capMatch = p.title.match(/(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*(TB|GB)\b/i);
  const capTB = capMatch ? (capMatch[2].toUpperCase()==='TB' ? parseFloat(capMatch[1]) : parseFloat(capMatch[1])/1000) : null;
  return {...p, capacity: capMatch ? capMatch[0].toUpperCase() : '', capacityTB: capTB};
});
const filteredMC = parsedMC.filter(p => p.capacityTB !== null && p.capacityTB > 2).sort((a,b)=>(a.price??999999)-(b.price??999999));
console.log(JSON.stringify({currentUrl: location.href, pageCounts:[productsPage1MC.length, productsPage2MC.length], total: allProductsMC.length, filteredCount: filteredMC.length, filters: await page.evaluate(()=>Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('a')).map(a=>a.textContent?.trim().replace(/\s+/g,' ')).filter(t=>['external hard drive','External Hard Drives','Mac'].includes(t))), products: filteredMC}, null, 2));
</request>
